740    3400   0   0 194  10 0 "Default Font"
do not have a specific mux position in
760    3190   0   0 194  10 0 "Default Font"
this device.
740    2750   0   0 194  10 0 "Default Font"
In this controlCARD, a standard GPIO
740    2550   0   0 194  10 0 "Default Font"
is used to detect changes to these
740    2350   0   0 194  10 0 "Default Font"
signals.
730    1870   0   0 194  10 0 "Default Font"
R83 is populated to allow a customer to
730    1680   0   0 194  10 0 "Default Font"
evaluate the controlCARD without a 
740    1500   0   0 194  10 0 "Default Font"
baseboard if they desire.  USB specifies the
750    1310   0   0 194  10 0 "Default Font"
total bus capacitance on any device as 10uF
750    1130   0   0 194  10 0 "Default Font"
max.  R83 should be depopulated in most
750    930    0   0 194  10 0 "Default Font"
end applications.
